exercise 
of

through its P & GS Department, Chennai for the period 
from 6th February 2019 to 31st December 2020.

No.II(2)/HWMP/279/2019.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule 
below have to be acquired for highways purpose, to wit 
for development of Tiruchengode  to Namakkal State 
Highways Road to four laning at Namakkal District and 
it having already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out 
of the funds controlled or managed by the Chief Engineer 
(Construction 
& 
Maintenance), 
Highways 
Department, 
Chennai-25 and after having considered the cause  shown 
by the owners or other persons having interest in the 
said lands as the case may be do hereby publish the 
following notice under Sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) 
NOTICE
Under 
sub-section 
(1) 
of 
Section 
15 
of 
the
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 
2002), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the 
lands speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below measuring, an extent 
of  675.5 Sq.mts  of   Dry and Natham Lands to the 
same, a little more or less needed for Highways purpose, 
to wit, for development of Tiruchengode to Namakkal State 
Highways in Namakkal District. The Plan of the lands are 
kept in the oﬃ  ce of the District Collector, Namakkal and 
may be inspected at any time during oﬃ  ce hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/280/2019.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in schedule 
below  and situated in the Village Kasinayakanpatti in the 
Taluk of Tirupattur in the District of Vellore are needed 
for Highways purpose to wit  for construction of Tirupattur 
By-pass Road and it having already been decided that 
the entire amount of compensation  to be awarded 
for the lands is to be paid by the Divisional Engineer 
(NABARD 
& 
Rural 
Roads), 
Highways 
Department, 
Vellore, 
 
after 
considering 
the 
cause 
shown 
by 
the 
owner 
or 
other 
persons 
having 
interest 
on 
such lands, as the case may, do here by publish the 
following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil  Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 
2002).
NOTICE

sub-section 
(1) 
of 
Section 
15 
of 
the 
Tamil 
Nadu 
Highways Act, 
2001 
(Tamil 
Nadu Act,
34 of 2002), the Governor of Tamil Nadu here by acquires 
the lands speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below measuring 4780 Sq. 
Meters needed for Highways  the purpose to wit for formation 
of Tirupattur By-pass Road.
The plan of the lands is kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Tahsildar, 
Tirupattur, Vellore District and may be inspected at any 
time during oﬃ  ce hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/282/2019.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule 
below have to be acquired for highways purpose, to wit 
for formation of By-Pass road to Tiruchengode Town at 
Namakkal District and it having already been decided that 
the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed 
by the Chief Engineer (NABARD & Rural Roads), Highways 
Department, Chennai-25 and after having considered the 
cause shown by the owners or other persons having interest 
in the said lands as the case may be do hereby publish, 
the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 
of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands speciﬁ ed in the 
Schedule below measuring, an extent of 1.76.87 Hectare 
of Ryotwari dry lands to the same, a little more or less 
needed for Highways purpose, to wit for the formation of 
By-Pass Road to Tiruchengode Town in Namakkal District. 
The Plan of the lands are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the District 
Collector, Namakkal and may be inspected at any time 
during oﬃ  ce hours.

Namakkal  District, Tiruchengode Taluk, 37. Andipalayam Village.

No.II(2)/HWMP/283/2019.—The Governor  of Tamil Nadu 
having been  satisﬁ ed  that the  lands  speciﬁ ed  in the 
schedule  below have to be acquired  for Highways  purpose 
for the formation of By-pass Road  to Tiruvannamalai Town 
starting  from Cuddalore-Chittoor Road Km. 112/4 and ending 
at Km. 112/6 in  connection  with   National Highways 66 
in Tiruvannamalai District and it has already been decided 
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded 
for the lands is to be paid  out of the funds  controlled 
or managed  by the Divisional  Engineer (NABARD and 
Rural Roads), Highways  Department,  Vellore District  after 
considering  the cause shown  by the owner (or) other 
person having  interest on such lands as the case may 
be hereby publish the following notice under sub-section 
(1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu  Highways Act, 2001 
(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu  hereby acquires the land speciﬁ ed  in the 
schedule below measuring  to an extent of 12797 Square 
meters of dry lands  in Survey No. 1/1A1  etc., in Vengikkal 
Village,  Triuvannamalai Taluk,  and District to the same 
a little more or less needed for the formation of By-Pass 
Road to Tiruvannamalai Town starting from Cuddalore-Chittor 
Road Km. 112/4 and ending at Km. 112/6 in connection 
with National Highways 66 in Tiruvannamalai District.
The Plan of the lands is kept in Taluk Oﬃ  ce, 
Tiruvannamalai and may be inspected at any time during 
oﬃ  ce hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ

No.II(2)/HWMP/285/2019.—The 
Governor 
of
Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in 
the schedule below have to be acquired for Highways purpose 
for the formation of By-pass Road to Tiruvannamalai Town 
starting from Cuddalore- Chittoor Road Km 112/4 and ending 
at Km 112/6 in connection with National Highways 66 in 
Tiruvannamalai District and it has already been decided that 
the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands 
is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the 
Divisional Engineer (NABARD and Rural Roads), Highways 
Department, Vellore District after considering the cause 
shown by the owner (or) other person having interest on such 
lands as the case may be hereby publish the following notice 
under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under Sub Section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land speciﬁ ed in the 
schedule below measuring to an extent of 16563 Square 
meter of dry lands in Survey No. 108/4 etc., in Devanandal 
Village, Tiruvannamalai Taluk and District to the same a little 
more or less needed for the formation of By-pass road to 
Tiruvannamalai Town starting from Cuddalore-Chittor Road 
Km 112/4 and ending at Km. 112/6 in connection with 
National Highways 66 in Tiruvannamalai District.
The Plan of the lands is kept in Taluk Office, 
Tiruvannamalai and may be inspected at any time during 
oﬃ  ce hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Tiruvannamalai District, Tiruvannamalai Taluk, 31. Devanandal Village.

[G.O. (2D) No.21, Highways and Minor Ports (HQ2), 
5th March 2019, ñ£C 21, M÷‹H, F¼õœÀõ˜   Ý‡´-2050.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/287/2019.—The  Governor  of Tamil Nadu 
having been  satisﬁ ed  that the  lands  speciﬁ ed  in the 
schedule  below have to be acquired  for Highways  purpose 
for the Formation of By-Pass Road  to  Tiruvannamalai 
Town  starting  from Cuddalore – Chittoor Road Km 112/4 
and ending  at Km 112/6 in  connection  with   National 
Highways 66 in Tiruvannamalai District, and it has already 
been decided that the entire amount of compensation 
to be awarded for the lands is to be paid  out of the 
funds  controlled or managed  by the Divisional  Engineer, 
Nabard and Rural Roads, Highways  Department, Vellore 
District  after considering  the cause shown  by the owner 
(or) other person having  interest on such lands as the 
case may be hereby publish the following notice under
sub section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu  Highways 
Act, 2001  (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE 
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of  2002) the 
Governor  of Tamil Nadu  hereby acquires  the land 
specified  in the schedule  below measuring  to an 
extent of  17982  Square meter  of dry lands  in Survey
No. 2/2A etc in Athiyandal  Village,  Triuvannamalai Taluk 
and District to the same a little more or less needed for 
the formation of By-Pass Road to Tiruvannamalai Town 
starting from Cuddalore - Chittor Road Km 112/4 and ending 
at  Km. 112/6 in connection with National Highways  66 
in Tiruvannamalai District.
The Plan of the lands is kept in Taluk Office, 
Tiruvannamalai and may be inspected at any time during 
oﬃ  ce hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/288/2019.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in schedule 
below and situated in the Village 11. Achamangalam in the 
Taluk of Tirupattur in the District of Vellore  are needed 
for Highways purpose to wit  for formation of Tirupattur 
By-Pass Road and it having already been decided that 
the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
lands is to be paid by the Divisional Engineer (NABARD 
and Rural Roads), Highways Department, Vellore, after 
considering the cause shown by the owner or other 
persons having interest on such lands, as the case may, 
do here by publish the following notice under sub-section 
(1) of Section 15 of the Tamil  Nadu Highways Act 2001
(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) 
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act 2001(Tamil Nadu Act-34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu here by acquires the lands speciﬁ ed in the 
Schedule below measuring   62661 Sq. Meters needed for 
Highways  the purpose to wit for formation  of Tirupattur 
By-Pass Road.
The plan of the lands is kept in the oﬃ  ce of the 
Tahsildar, Tirupattur, Vellore District and may be inspected 
at any time during oﬃ  ce hours.

Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu here by acquires the land speciﬁ ed in the 
schedule below measuring an extent of 3.96.51 Hectares

No.II(2)/HWMP/290/2019.—The Governor of
Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands in the schedule 
below and situated in the Thiruvanmiyur Town, Block No.28, 
29, 30, 36, 37, 38, 39, 40, 41, 42, 44 and45 are required 
for Highways purpose i.e., for Widening And Strengthening 
Of Six Laning Of East Coast Road from Thiruvanmiyur To 
Akkarai Village under Chennai Metropolitan Development 
Project Division-I, Guindy, Chennai-32 and it having already 
been decided that the entire amount of Compensation to 
be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds 
controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, (Metro) 
Highways Department, Alandur, Chennai-16 and after having 
considered the cause shown by the owner or other person 
having interest in the said lands, as the case may be, 
do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section 
(1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001
(TN Act 34/2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (TN Act 34/2002). 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land 
speciﬁ ed in the schedule below measuring an extent of 
12255.94 Sq.Mtr. to the same, a little more or less required 
for Highways purpose i.e., for Widening and Strengthening 
of Six Laning of East Coast Road from Thiruvanmiyur to 
Akkarai Village under Chennai Metropolitan Development 
Project Division-I, Guindy Chennai-32.
The plan of the land under acquisition kept in the Oﬃ  ce 
of the Special Deputy Collector (L.A), Tamil Nadu Urban 
Development Project, Metro, Alandur, Chennai-16 and may 
be inspected at any time during oﬃ  ce hours.

HOME DEPARTMENT
Transfer the case registered in Dharmapuri District Crime 
Branch in Crime No.09/2017 under Sections 409, 420, 
423, 467, 468, 477(A) Indian Penal Code to the Economic 
Oﬀ ences Wing, Central Bureau of Investigation, Rajaji 
Bhavan, Besent Nagar, Chennai for further investigation 
by issuing a notiﬁ cation under Section 6 of the Delhi 
Special Police Establishment Act.
[G.O. Ms. No.154, Home (Police-XIV), 7th March 2019.]
No.II(2)/HO/291/2019.—Under Section 6 of the Delhi 
Special Police Establishment Act, 1946 (Central Act 25 of 
1946), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby accord his consent 
to the extension of the powers and jurisdiction of members 
of the Delhi Special Police Establishment in the whole of 
the State of Tamil Nadu to investigate the case registered 
in Dharmapuri District Crime Branch in Crime No.09/2017 
under Sections 409, 420, 423, 467, 468 and 477(A) of the 
Indian Penal Code (Central Act XLV of 1860).
 
NIRANJAN  MARDI,

LATE NOTIFICATION:
NOTIFICATION BY GOVERNMENT
HOME DEPARTMENT
(SC)
Award of the Fire Service Medal for Meritorious 
Service on the Occasion of the Republic Day, 2019.
[Letter No.HSC.1/546-8/2018, Home (S.C), 
25th March 2019.]

Government of India Presidents Secretariat New Delhi, the 
26th January 2019 is republished:—
No.15-Pres/2019—The President is pleased on the 
occasion of the Republic Day, 2019 to award the Fire 
Service Medal for Meritorious Service to the under mentioned 
oﬃ  cers:-
